country_event = {
	id = hellas.1
	title = hellas.1.t
	desc = hellas.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bloody_may_thess
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
    timeout_days = 4

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
			goto_province = 11818
            set_country_flag = GRE_strikes_dealt
            clr_country_flag = GRE_strikes_started
        }
    }
	
	#Give into Greece
	option = {
		name = hellas.1.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }

		GRE = {
            add_stability = 0.35
            add_war_support = 0.3
            add_to_variable = { fct_mon = 5}   
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_com = 7.5}
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_dem = 5}
            add_to_variable = { fct_fas = 5}
            set_variable = { decision_taken = 0 }
            set_variable = { metaxas_pro_axis = 1 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
            hidden_effect = { complete_national_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes }
		}
    }
	option = {
		name = hellas.1.b

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
        }

		GRE = {
            add_stability = 0.15
            add_war_support = 0.1
            add_to_variable = { fct_mon = 2.5}   
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_com = 1.5}
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_dem = 1.0}
            add_to_variable = { fct_fas = 2.5}
            set_variable = { decision_taken = 1 }
            set_variable = { metaxas_pro_axis = 0.5 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
            hidden_effect = { complete_national_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes }
		}
    }
	option = {
		name = hellas.1.c

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
        }

		GRE = {
            add_stability = -0.15
            add_war_support = -0.05
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_mon = 2.5}   
            add_to_variable = { fct_com = 5}
            add_to_variable = { fct_dem = 2.5}
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_fas = 2.5}
            set_variable = { decision_taken = 2 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
            hidden_effect = { complete_national_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes }
		}
    }    
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.2
	title = hellas.2.t
	desc = hellas.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_metaxas

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.2.a

        add_stability = 0.02
        add_war_support = 0.15
        remove_country_leader_trait = greek_dictator
        add_country_leader_trait = arkhigos_0
        complete_national_focus = GRE_the_4th_of_august_regime
        set_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
        set_variable = { GRE_ark = 0 }
        if = { 
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 0 } } 
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon = 5}
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_com = -7.5}
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem = -7.5}
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_fas = 5}
            add_to_variable = { fct_mon = 5}   
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_com = 7.5}
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_dem = 7.5}
            add_to_variable = { fct_fas = 2.5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_papagos_selection_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = dem_fct_imp_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = com_fct_imp_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = fas_fct_imp_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = mon_fct_imp_tt 
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 1 } }
            add_to_variable = { fct_mon = 5}   
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_com = 7,5}
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_dem = 0}
            add_to_variable = { fct_fas = 1 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drakos_selection_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = fact_inf_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = com_fct_imp_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = mon_fct_imp_tt 
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 2 } }
            add_to_variable = { fct_mon = 2.5}   
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_com = 2.5}
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_dem = 2.5}
            add_to_variable = { fct_fas = 1 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_stanotas_selection_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = dem_fct_imp_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = com_fct_imp_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = mon_fct_imp_tt 
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 3 } }
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_mon = 2.5}   
            add_to_variable = { fct_dem = 2.5}
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_zervas_selection_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = dem_fct_imp_tt 
            custom_effect_tooltip = mon_fct_imp_tt 
        }
        faction_gui_call = yes   
        axal_gui_initial = yes 
        hidden_effect = { 
            add_ideas = GRE_kotzias
            add_ideas = GRE_diakos
        }
    }    
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.6
	title = hellas.6.t
	desc = hellas.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_red_dogs

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        date > 1936.08.01
		tag = GRE
        OR = {
    		check_variable = { var = fct_com value = 30 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = fct_dem value = 30 compare = less_than_or_equals }
        }
        has_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.6.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			}
        add_stability = -0.05
        if = { 
            limit = { check_variable = { var = fct_com value = 30 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
            set_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1
        }
        if = { 
            limit = { check_variable = { var = fct_dem value = 30 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
            set_country_flag = GRE_repub_upr_1
        }
    }
}

country_event = {               #IMRO GETS THE BOOT BY HAVING THE SLAVS CRUSHED (METAXAS DECISION)
	id = hellas.9
	title = hellas.9.t
	desc = hellas.9.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_greek_march

	trigger = {
		tag = GRE
        has_country_flag = BUL_imro_awakened_in_country_flag
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.9.a
        set_country_flag = BUL_repress_imro_flag
        clr_country_flag = BUL_repress_imro_flag
        clr_country_flag = BUL_imro_awakened_in_country_flag
        add_political_power = 150
        BUL = { add_political_power = -150 }
        every_controlled_state = { 
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = skirmishes_against_imro }
                }
            remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = skirmishes_against_imro }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = widespread_bulgarian_sentiment_01 }
                }
                remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = widespread_bulgarian_sentiment_01 }
            }
            remove_core_of = BUL
            add_core_of = ROOT
        }     
    }    
}

            reduce_unpreparedness = yes

	id = hellas.201

	desc = hellas.201.desc

	trigger = {
		tag = GRE
        date < 1942.1.1
        NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended }
        ITA = { 
            exists = yes 
            is_puppet = no
            is_subject = no
            NOT = { 
                is_justifying_wargoal_against = GRE 
                has_war_with = GRE

                    focus = ITA_greece_war_goal
                    progress > 0.01
                }
            }
            has_government = fascism
            has_country_leader = {
                name = "Benito Mussolini"
                ruling_only = yes 
            }
        }
        ALB = {
            OR = {
                exists = no
                AND = { 
                    exists = yes 
                    OR = {
                        is_subject_of = ITA
                        is_puppet_of = ITA 
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        divisions_in_border_state = {
            type = infantry
            size > 2
            state = 185
            border_state = 805
        }      
        divisions_in_border_state = {
            type = infantry
            size > 2

country_event = {               #WARNING EVENT FOR TOO MANY DIVISIONS DEPLOYED (BASED ON ITA'S INTEL ON YOU)
	id = hellas.202
	title = hellas.202.t
	desc = hellas.202.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_italian_rise2

	trigger = {
		tag = GRE
        has_war = no
        date < 1942.1.1
        NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended }
        ITA = {
            exists = yes 
            is_puppet = no
            is_subject = no
            NOT = {
                has_completed_focus = ITA_greece_war_goal
                has_completed_focus = ITA_greece_friend
                focus_progress = {
                    focus = ITA_greece_war_goal
                    progress > 0.01
                }
                is_justifying_wargoal_against = GRE
                has_war_with = GRE
            }
            has_government = fascism
            has_country_leader = {
                name = "Benito Mussolini"
                ruling_only = yes 
            }
        }
        ALB = {
            OR = {
                exists = no
                AND = { 
                    exists = yes 
                    OR = {
                        is_subject_of = ITA
                        is_puppet_of = ITA 
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { x = ITA.army_intel@GRE }                              ### FORMULA: y = -0.25x + 30 where y the num of divisions and x the army intel italy has over greece (5,30 min-max)
        multiply_temp_variable = { x = -0.25 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = 30 }
        num_divisions > x
		date > 1936.08.04
        has_country_leader = {
            name = "Ioannis Metaxas"
            ruling_only = yes
        }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
    
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.202.a
        activate_mission = GRE_activated_mission_2
    }      
}

	id = hellas.203
	title = hellas.203.t
	desc = hellas.203.desc

	trigger = {
        original_tag = GRE 
        check_variable = { preparedness_level < 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { x = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
        check_variable = { x > eq_thr?10000 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
    
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { evnt_cnt_203 = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { eq_thr?10000 = 5000 }
        }
    }
    
	option = {
		name = hellas.203.a
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { evnt_cnt_203 = 1 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_25_percent_of_lvl3_generals_tt
        }
        else = {
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_percent_in_order_generals_tt
        }
        hidden_effect = { activate_decision = hidden_proc_for_equip_event }
    }      
}

unit_leader_event = {                                                                   #Untrained Officer Dies 
	id = hellas.236
	title = hellas.236.t
	desc = hellas.236.desc
    is_triggered_only = yes 

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            THIS = {
                remove_unit_leader = yes
                add_to_variable = { GRE.officers_died = 1 }
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.236.a
    }
}

unit_leader_event = {                                                                   #Untrained Officer Critically Wounded 
	id = hellas.237
	title = hellas.237.t
	desc = hellas.237.desc
    is_triggered_only = yes 

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            THIS = {
                add_timed_unit_leader_trait = {
                    trait = gre_critically_wounded
                    days = 45
                }
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.237.a
    }
}

unit_leader_event = {                                                                   #Officer Defects
	id = hellas.238
	title = hellas.238.t
	desc = hellas.238.desc
    is_triggered_only = yes 

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            THIS = {
                remove_unit_leader = yes
                add_to_variable = { GRE.officers_defected = 1 }
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.238.a
        trigger = {
            THIS = { is_general_undesired = no}
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.238.b
        trigger = {
            THIS = {
                is_general_undesired = yes
                has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_communist_persona
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.238.c
        trigger = {
            THIS = {
                is_general_undesired = yes
                has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_republican_persona
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.238.d
        trigger = {
            THIS = {
                is_general_undesired = yes
                has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_fascist_persona
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.238.3
        trigger = {
            THIS = {
                is_general_undesired = yes
                has_trait = trait_gre_stauch_monarchist_persona
            }
        }
    }

state_event = {                                                                        # Mining Rights Events
	id = hellas.241
	title = hellas.241.t
	desc = hellas.241.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_bank_of_greece
	is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ###[State Temp Variables]###
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_oil = resource@oil }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_aluminium = resource@aluminium }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_rubber = resource@rubber }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_tungsten = resource@tungsten }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_steel = resource@steel }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_chromium = resource@chromium }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_id = THIS.id}
            every_country = {
                limit = { is_influencable = yes is_major = yes num_of_military_factories>20 num_of_civilian_factories>20 has_capitulated = no }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_oil > 0 } }
                    ###[Oil]###
                    if = { limit = { OR = { original_tag = GER original_tag = JAP original_tag = ITA } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.25 } }
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@oil }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@oil }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { fuel_available = produces }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                check_variable = { fuel_available < 75 }
                                fuel_ratio < 0.41
                            }
                        }
                        multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.25 }
                    }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_aluminium > 0 } }
                    ###[Aluminium]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@aluminium }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@aluminium }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { aluminium_available = produces }                          ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { aluminium_required = THIS.resource_consumed@aluminium }   ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { aluminium_required > aluminium_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_rubber > 0 } }
                    ###[Rubber]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@rubber }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@rubber }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { rubber_available = produces }                             ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { rubber_required = THIS.resource_consumed@rubber }         ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { rubber_required > rubber_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_tungsten > 0 } }
                    ###[Tungsten]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@tungsten }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@tungsten }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { tungsten_available = produces }                           ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { tungsten_required = THIS.resource_consumed@tungsten }     ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { tungsten_required > tungsten_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_steel > 0 } }
                    ###[Steel]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@steel }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@steel }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { steel_available = produces }                              ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { steel_required = THIS.resource_consumed@steel }           ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { steel_required > steel_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_chromium > 0 } }
                    ###[Chromium]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@chromium }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@chromium }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { chromium_available = produces }                           ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { chromium_required = THIS.resource_consumed@chromium }     ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { chromium_required > chromium_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                add_to_array = { GRE.h241_id = THIS.id }
                add_to_array = { GRE.h241_weight = h241_needed_weight }
                clear_variable = h241_needed_weight
            }
        }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.241.a
        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.242 days = 0 } }
    }
}

country_event = {               #MINING RIGHTS - RETURN EVENT
	id = hellas.242
	title = hellas.242.t
	desc = hellas.242.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_variable = { iterations = h241_id^num }
            while_loop_effect = {
                break = br
                limit = { always = yes }
                
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { h241_id^num = 0 } } set_temp_variable = { br = 1 } }
                else = {
                    find_highest_in_array = { array = h241_weight value = val_highest index = idx_highest }
                    add_to_array = { h241_sorted_weight = val_highest }
                    add_to_array = { h241_sorted_id = h241_id^idx_highest }
                    remove_from_array = { array = h241_weight index = idx_highest }
                    remove_from_array = { array = h241_id index = idx_highest }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^0 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^0 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^0 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^1 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^1 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^1 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^2 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^2 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^2 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.e
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^3 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^3 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^3 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.f
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^4 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^4 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^4 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.g
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^5 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^5 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^5 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.h
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^6 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^6 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^6 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.i
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^7 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^7 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^7 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.j
        h241_clear_variables = yes
    }

country_event = {               #MINING RIGHTS - FINAL PART A
	id = hellas.243
	title = hellas.243.t
	desc = hellas.243.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { check_variable = { h241_first_run = 0 } }
            hidden_effect = {
                ##################################[ State Calculators ]######################################
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_oil}                      # price = 0.2 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.2 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_aluminium}                # price = 0.08 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.08 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_rubber}                   # price = 0.18 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.18 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_tungsten}                 # price = 0.13 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.13 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_steel}                    # price = 0.10 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.1 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_chromium}                 # price = 0.07 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.07 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                multiply_variable = { total_worth = h241_return_weight }
                round_variable = total_worth
                set_variable = { dec_pp_gain = 50 }
                multiply_variable = { dec_pp_gain = total_worth }
                set_variable = { dec_inf_equipment = total_worth }
                multiply_variable = { dec_inf_equipment = 500 }
                set_variable = { dec_art_equipment = total_worth }
                multiply_variable = { dec_art_equipment = 42 }
                set_variable = { dec_sup_equipment = total_worth }
                multiply_variable = { dec_sup_equipment = 45 }
                set_variable = { dec_factories_worth = total_worth }
                ##################################[ Recipient Willingness ]######################################
                set_variable = { h241_willingness = 1 }
                set_variable = { tmp_favor_multiplier = 1}
                random_country = {
                    limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                    set_temp_variable = { x = THIS.favor@GRE }
                }
                divide_temp_variable = { x = 100 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 1 }
                multiply_variable = { h241_willingness = x }
                calculate_alax_multiplier = yes
                multiply_variable = { h241_willingness = alax_multiplier }
                #################################################################################################
                add_to_variable = { h241_first_run = 1 }
            }
        }
    }

    #1. Political Power
    #2. Influence   ~Requires still influencable~
    #3. Equipment ~Requires not at war or at required in stockpile~
    #4. Diplomatic Support ~later on~
    #5. Country Specific Favors

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_pp_chosen = 0 } }
        effect_tooltip = { add_political_power = dec_pp_gain }
        set_variable = { dec_pp_chosen = 1 }
        #####################[Calculate Willingness Effects]############################
        random_country = {
            limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
            set_temp_variable = { x = political_power }
            set_temp_variable = { y = political_power_daily}
        }
        set_temp_variable = { z = dec_pp_gain }
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 2 }                # 50% of pp for check
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { x > z } }
            set_variable = { pp_willingness_cost = 0.5 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                multiply_temp_variable = { y = 180 }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { z = y }
                check_variable = { x > z }
            }
            set_variable = { pp_willingness_cost = 0.65 }
        }
        else = { set_variable = { pp_willingness_cost = 1.0 } }
        subtract_from_variable = { h241_willingness = pp_willingness_cost }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_pp_chosen > 0 } }
        add_to_variable = { h241_willingness = pp_willingness_cost }
        clear_variable = dec_pp_chosen
        clear_variable = pp_willingness_cost
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen = 0 } }
        effect_tooltip = {
            random_country = {
                limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = infantry_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_inf_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = support_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_sup_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = artillery_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_art_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { dec_equip_chosen = 1 }
        #####################[Calculate Willingness Effects]############################
        random_country = {
            limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
            set_temp_variable = { x1 = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
            set_temp_variable = { x2 = num_equipment@support_equipment }
            set_temp_variable = { x3 = num_equipment@artillery_equipment }
            set_temp_variable = { y1 = num_of_civilian_factories }
            set_temp_variable = { y2 = num_of_military_factories }          # base 4.5
            set_temp_variable = { y3 = num_of_factories }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { z = dec_inf_equipment }           # Take the guns
        divide_temp_variable = { z = y2 }                       # Divide by number of factories
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 0.5 }                      # Divide by 2 to simulate half Mils taken (not 100%)
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 180 }                      # Divide by number of days they will gain rights. We got cost/day.
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 4.5 }                      # Divide by 4.5 to gain x.xxx based percentage of factory capabilities
        if = {
            limit = { has_war = yes OR = { check_variable = { x1 < 1 } check_variable = { x2 < 1 } check_variable = { x3 < 1 } } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 5 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_war = no check_variable = { x1 < 1 } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 2.5 }
            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_war = no check_variable = { x1 > 0 } check_variable = { x1 < var:dec_inf_equipment } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 2.0 }
            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_war = no NOT = { check_variable = { x1 < var:dec_inf_equipment } } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 1.25 }
            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        subtract_from_variable = { h241_willingness = eq_willingness_cost }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.d
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen > 0 } }
        clear_variable = dec_equip_chosen
        add_to_variable = { h241_willingness = eq_willingness_cost }
        clear_variable = eq_willingness_cost
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.e
        country_event = { id = hellas.245 days = 0 }
    }
}

            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        subtract_from_variable = { h241_willingness = eq_willingness_cost }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.244.d
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen > 0 } }
        clear_variable = dec_equip_chosen
        add_to_variable = { h241_willingness = eq_willingness_cost }
        clear_variable = eq_willingness_cost
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.244.e
        country_event = { id = hellas.245 days = 0 }
    }
}

country_event = {               #MINING RIGHTS - ACCEPTED OR DENIED
	id = hellas.245
	title = hellas.245.t
	desc = hellas.245.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no


    option = {                                                  ## Accepted
        trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { h241_willingness < 0 } } }
        name = hellas.245.a
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { dec_pp_chosen > 0 } }
            add_political_power = var:dec_pp_gain
            set_temp_variable = { x = var:dec_pp_gain }
            multiply_temp_variable = { x = -1 }
            random_country = {
                limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                add_political_power = x
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen > 0 } }
            random_country = {
                limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = infantry_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_inf_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = support_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_sup_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = artillery_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_art_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
            }
        }
        random_country = {
            limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
            GRE = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = PREV state = var:GRE.h241_state_id } }
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            random_state = {
                limit = { state = var:GRE.h241_state_id }
                set_state_flag = given_mining_rights
                set_variable = { return_owner = GRE.h241_return_id }
            }
            h241_clear_variables = yes
        }
    }

    option = {                                                  ## Rejected
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_willingness < 0 } }
        name = hellas.245.b
        h241_clear_variables = yes
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                           ### Balkan Pact Ultimatum to Bulgarians (tag = BUL)
	id = hellas.3200
	title = hellas.3200.t
	desc = hellas.3200.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_metaxas_inonu_balkan_leaders

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                                              ### Bulgaria accepts
		name = hellas.3200.a    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
        BUL = {
            clr_country_flag = channels_established
            set_country_flag = common_strategy_with_greece_defined 
            add_opinion_modifier = { 
                target = GRE
                modifier = GRE_common_balkan_strategy
            }
            set_country_flag = common_strategy_with_greece_defined
        }
        GRE = {
            add_opinion_modifier = { 
                target = BUL
                modifier = GRE_common_balkan_strategy
            }
            country_event = { id = hellas.3201 days = 1 }
        }
        every_state = {
            limit = {
                has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged }
            }
            remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged }
        }
    }  
	option = {                                                                                               ### Bulgaria Declines
		name = hellas.3200.b    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GRE
					ratio > 1.25
				}
                strength_ratio = {
					tag = YUG
					ratio > 1.25
				}
                strength_ratio = {
					tag = ROM
					ratio > 1.25
				}
			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                set_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = GRE.num_battalions }
                add_to_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = YUG.num_battalions }
                add_to_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = ROM.num_battalions }
                add_to_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = TUR.num_battalions }
                divide_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = BUL.num_battalions }
                check_variable = { manpower_sum < 2.5 }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 3
                check_variable = { BUL.favor@GRE < -30 }
            }
		}
        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.3202 days = 1 } }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                           ### Germans on Intervention
	id = hellas.3203
	title = {
        text = hellas.3203.a.t 
        trigger = { 
            OR = {
                check_variable = { GER.favor@GRE > 89 }
                has_country_flag = GRE_axis_rallied_against_bulgarians
                has_country_flag = GRE_requested_axis_support_over_the_bulgarian_matter
            }
        }
    }
    title = {
        text = hellas.3203.b.t 
        trigger = { 
            NOT = {
                check_variable = { GER.favor@GRE > 89 }
                has_country_flag = GRE_axis_rallied_against_bulgarians
                has_country_flag = GRE_requested_axis_support_over_the_bulgarian_matter
            }
        }
    }
	desc = hellas.3203.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_diplomacy

	trigger = {
        original_tag = GRE
        has_decision = push_for_bulgarian_entry_in_the_balkan_pact
    }

	fire_only_once = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        check_variable = { GER.favor@GRE > 89 }
                        has_country_flag = GRE_axis_rallied_against_bulgarians
                        has_country_flag = GRE_requested_axis_support_over_the_bulgarian_matter
                        set_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = GRE.num_battalions }
                        add_to_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = YUG.num_battalions }
                        add_to_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = ROM.num_battalions }
                        add_to_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = TUR.num_battalions }
                        divide_temp_variable = { manpower_sum = BUL.num_battalions }
                        check_variable = { manpower_sum > 8 }
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = { BUL = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
                    BUL = { 
                        leave_faction = yes 
                        set_rule = { can_join_factions = no }
                    }
                }
                every_country = {
                    limit = { NOT = { original_tag = ITA } has_guaranteed = BUL }
                    diplomatic_relation = {
                        country = BUL
                        relation = guarantee
                        active = no
                    }
                }
                GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.3204 days = 2 } }
            }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.3203.a
    }
}

                    #	retire_ideology_leader = fascism
                    #}

            }

country_event = {                               # BRITISH DEAL
	id = hellas.3182
	title = hellas.3182.t
	desc = hellas.3182.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_trade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {  ### BRITAIN ACCEPTS
		name = hellas.3182.a    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
        GRE = { add_political_power = 300 }
        add_political_power = 75
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = guarantee
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        GRE = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = ENG
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            } 
        }
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = docking_rights
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        GRE = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = ENG
                relation = docking_rights
                active = yes
            }  
        }
        ### THE FOLLOWING BLOCK ADDS A MASSIVE BOOST OF FAVOR TO UK AND THEIR ALLIES. LIKEWISE SUBTRACTS A MASSIVE AMOUNT OF FAVOR FROM THEIR ENEMIES.
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = {
                        array = global.favor_mechanic
                        value = THIS.id
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            is_in_faction_with = ENG
                            AND = {
                                original_tag = USA
                                has_government = democratic
                                ENG = { has_government = democratic }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 30 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            original_tag = GER
                            original_tag = ITA
                            original_tag = BUL
                        }
                        NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            original_tag = GER
                        }
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 20 } 
                    }
                    else = {
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 30 }   
                    } 
                }
            } 
        }
        news_event = { id = hellenic_news.200 days = 0 }
    }  
	option = {  ### BRITAIN DECLINES
		name = hellas.3182.b    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
			}
		}        
        GRE = { add_political_power = 150 }  
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = {
                        array = global.favor_mechanic
                        value = THIS.id
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            is_in_faction_with = ENG
                            AND = {
                                original_tag = USA
                                has_government = democratic
                                ENG = { has_government = democratic }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 5 }
                }
            }
        }        
    }     
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.350
	title = hellas.350.t
	desc = hellas.350.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_maniadakis_rounding_up

	trigger = {
        has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr
        NOT = { has_country_flag = com_civilwar_started }
        check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr < 120 }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 160
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { cnt = amount_of_work_in_asfaleia }
            set_temp_variable = { final = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { weight = 0.05 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { weight = cnt }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { final = weight }
            factor = final
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr < 181 }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.25
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr > 180 }
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.350.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }
        add_days_mission_timeout = {
            mission = GRE_comm_upr
            days = 30
        }
    }  
}

	trigger = {
        has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr
        NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }
        check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_repub_upr < 120 }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 160
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { cnt = amount_of_work_in_asfaleia }
            set_temp_variable = { final = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { weight = 0.05 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { weight = cnt }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { final = weight }
            factor = final
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_repub_upr < 181 }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.25
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_repub_upr > 180 }
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.350.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }
        add_days_mission_timeout = {
            mission = GRE_repub_upr
            days = 30
        }
    }
}

        NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 1
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { x = 3.75 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { x = fct_dem }
            add_to_temp_variable = { x = 10 }
            factor = x
            always = yes
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.352.a

		ai_chance = {base = 100}
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_increase = 0.10 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_up_dem
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_over_200_danger_tt
        GRE_faction_refresh = yes
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.354
	title = hellas.354.t
	desc = hellas.354.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_civil_war_greek

	trigger = {
        original_tag = GRE
        OR = {
            AND = {
                NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = mon_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_mon < 20 }
            }
            AND = {
                has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr
                NOT = { has_government = democratic }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = republican_uprising_utterly_crushed }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_dem < 20 }
            }
            AND = {
                has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr
                NOT = { has_government = communism }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = communist_uprising_utterly_crushed }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = com_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_com_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_com < 20 }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { has_government = fascism }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = fas_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_fas_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_fas < 20 }
            }
        }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.354.a

		if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = mon_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_mon < 20 }
            }
            set_temp_variable = { x = party_popularity@neutrality }
            start_civil_war = {
                ruling_party = ROOT
                ideology = neutrality
                size = x
                capital = 47
                states = { 
                    807 186 187
                }
                keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                    has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_monarchist_persona
                }
                keep_political_leader = yes
            }
            set_country_flag = mon_civilwar_started
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_government = democratic }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = republican_uprising_utterly_crushed }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_dem < 20 }
            }
            set_temp_variable = { x = party_popularity@democratic }
            start_civil_war = {
                ruling_party = ROOT
                ideology = democratic
                size = x
                capital = 47
                states = {
                    811 731 810 812
                }
                keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                    has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_republican_persona
                }
                keep_political_leader = yes
            }
            set_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_government = communism }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = communist_uprising_utterly_crushed }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = com_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_com_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_com < 20 }
            }
            set_temp_variable = { x = party_popularity@communism }
            start_civil_war = {
                ruling_party = ROOT
                ideology = communism
                size = x
                capital = 47
                states = {
                    185 809 810
                }
                keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                    has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_communist_persona
                }
                keep_political_leader = yes
            }
            set_country_flag = com_civilwar_started
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_government = fascism }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = fas_civilwar_started }
                check_variable = { fct_fas_effect_multiplier > 1.99 }
                check_variable = { fct_fas < 20 }

            set_temp_variable = { x = party_popularity@fascism }

country_event = {       ## Choose Partner to Modernize the army
	id = hellas.405
	title = hellas.405.t
	desc = hellas.405.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {  ##ENG/FRA
		name = hellas.405.a
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = FRA.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
        }     
        hidden_effect = {
            ### MOTORIZED / MECH1 ###
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = motorised_infantry } }
                set_technology = { motorised_infantry = 1 }
            }
            ########################
            ###       TANKS      ###
            set_technology = { gwtank = 1 }
            set_technology = { basic_heavy_tank = 1 }
            ########################
            ###      SUPPORT     ###
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_engineers2 } }
                set_technology = { tech_engineers2 = 1 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_recon2 } }
                set_technology = { tech_recon2 = 1 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_maintenance_company } }
                set_technology = { tech_maintenance_company = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_maintenance_company2 } }
                set_technology = { tech_maintenance_company2 = 1 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_field_hospital } }
                set_technology = { tech_field_hospital = 1 }
            }  
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_field_hospital2 } }
                set_technology = { tech_field_hospital2 = 1 }
            } 
            ########################
            ###      WEAPONS     ###
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = infantry_weapons1 } }
                set_technology = { infantry_weapons1 = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = infantry_weapons2 } }
                set_technology = { infantry_weapons2 = 1 }
            }  
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons } }
                set_technology = { improved_infantry_weapons = 1 }
            }  
            ########################
            ###     ARTILLERY    ###
            #ART
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = interwar_artillery } }
                set_technology = { interwar_artillery = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = artillery1 } }
                set_technology = { artillery1 = 1 }
            }  
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = artillery2 } }
                set_technology = { artillery2 = 1 }
            } 
            #AA
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = antiair1 } }
                set_technology = { antiair1 = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = antiair2 } }
                set_technology = { antiair2 = 1 }
            }  
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = antiair3 } }
                set_technology = { antiair3 = 1 }
            }  
            #AT
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = antitank1 } }
                set_technology = { antitank1 = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = antitank2 } }
                set_technology = { antitank2 = 1 }
            }  
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = antitank3 } }
                set_technology = { antitank3 = 1 }
            }            
            ########################
            ###     DOCTRINE     ###
            add_tech_bonus = {
                name = GRE_modernize_the_army
                bonus = 4.0
                uses = 2
                category = cat_grand_battle_plan
            }        
        }        
    }

		name = hellas.405.b
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }

            }

                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = mechanised_infantry } }
                set_technology = { mechanised_infantry = 1 }        
            }

            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = armored_car1 } }
                set_technology = { armored_car1 = 1 }

                set_technology = { armored_car2 = 1 }

country_event = {                                                                                   ## Italian Stance
	id = hellas.407
	title = hellas.407.t
	desc = {
        text = hellas.407_neutral.desc
        trigger = { ITA = { contingency_threshold_reached = yes } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.407_negative.desc
        trigger = { ITA = { contingency_threshold_reached = no } }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_mussolini_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.407.a
        if = { 
            limit = { ITA = { contingency_threshold_reached = no } NOT = { is_in_array = { array = global.contingency_enemies value = ITA.id } } }
            add_to_array = { global.contingency_enemies = ITA.id }
        }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.500
	title = hellas.500.t
	desc = hellas.500.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.500.a #small investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 30 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 30 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 4
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 8 
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GRE_small_investment
			days = 30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GRE = {
				country_event = { id = hellas.501 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = hellas.500.b #no investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		GRE = { 
			country_event = { id = hellas.502 days = 2 }
		}
	}	
}

country_event = {                                                                           ### - Mediocre Investment
	id = hellas.503
	title = hellas.503.t
	desc = hellas.503.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
    
	option = {
		name = hellas.503.a #medium investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 30 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.5
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 30 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 8 
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GRE_moderate_investment
			days = 30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GRE = {
				country_event = { id = hellas.504 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = hellas.503.b #no investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		GRE = { 
			country_event = { id = hellas.502 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}


### -> Expand Mines (limited times, offers an influence boost)
### -> Substantial building slot expansion, additionally 1+1 factory.
### -> Oil drilling (ONCE - country chosen gets influence boost)
### -> Outsourcing (grants off-map factories but cancels when at war or allied with opponents)

country_event = {                                                                           ### - Greece receives mediocre Investment
	id = hellas.504
	title = hellas.504.t
	desc = hellas.504.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
    
	option = {                                                                                  ### Opening up the Land
		name = hellas.504.a #medium investment
        if = {                                                                              
            limit = {
                FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = ENG
                        original_tag = USA
                        original_tag = FRA
                    }
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_extra_slots_per_manpower_better_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                every_owned_state = {   
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 400
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 800
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    } 
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 1200
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
                    }   
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 2000
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
                    }  
                    else = {
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 5
                    }            
                }
            }
        }
        else = {
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_extra_slots_per_manpower_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                every_owned_state = {   
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 400
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 0
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 800
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
                    } 
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 1200
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    }   
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 2000
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
                    }  
                    else = {
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
                    }            
                }    
            }
        }
    }
	option = {                                                                                  ### Outsourcing -> Leads to event below
		name = hellas.504.b #medium investment
        
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_outsourcing_tt
        country_event = { id = hellas.505 days = 0 }
    }
    
	option = {                                                                                  ### Oil Drilling
		name = hellas.504.c #medium investment
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE_drilled_for_oil value = 0 compare = equals }
        }
        if = {                                                                              
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_drilled_for_oil value = 0 compare = equals }
                FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = SOV
                        original_tag = USA
                    }
                }
            }
            187 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = oil
                    amount = 12
                }
            } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drilling_for_oil_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_drilled_for_oil = 1 }        
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_drilled_for_oil value = 0 compare = equals }
            }
            187 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = oil
                    amount = 8
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drilling_for_oil_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_drilled_for_oil = 1 }  
        }
    }
	option = {                                                                                  ### Expand Mines
		name = hellas.504.d #medium investment
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 2 compare = less_than_or_equals }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 0 compare = equals }
            }
            186 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 3
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = chromium
                    amount = 8
                }
            }
            47 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 4
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = tungsten
                    amount = 2
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_mine_expansion = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 1 compare = equals }
            }
            186 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 3
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = chromium
                    amount = 4
                }
            }
            47 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 2
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = tungsten
                    amount = 4
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_mine_expansion = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 2 compare = equals }
            }
            186 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 6
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = chromium
                    amount = 8
                }
            }
            47 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 6
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = tungsten
                    amount = 4
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_mine_expansion = 1 }
        }        
    }  
}

country_event = {                                                                           ### - Outsourcing -> Civs / Mils/ Docks
	id = hellas.505
	title = hellas.505.t
	desc = hellas.505.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
    
	option = {                                                                                  ### Civs
		name = hellas.505.a 
        if = {
            limit = {
                FROM.FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = ENG
                        original_tag = USA
                    }
                }
            }
            add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 2 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.civslent@GRE = 2 }
        }
        else = {
            add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.civslent@GRE = 1 }
        }
    }
    option = {                                                                                  ### Mils
		name = hellas.505.b
        if = {
            limit = {
                FROM.FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = GER
                        original_tag = SOV
                    }
                }
            }
            add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 2 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.milslent@GRE = 2 }
        }
        else = {
            add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.milslent@GRE = 1 }
        }
    }
    option = {                                                                                  ### Docs
		name = hellas.505.c
        if = {
            limit = {
                FROM.FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = ENG
                        original_tag = USA
                    }
                }
            }
            add_offsite_building = { type = dockyard level = 2 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.dockslent@GRE = 2 }
        }
        else = {
            add_offsite_building = { type = dockyard level = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.dockslent@GRE = 1 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                               ### Italy Starts Justifying Wargoal in any manner
	id = hellas.90
	title = hellas.90.t
	desc = hellas.90.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_mussolini_diplomacy

    trigger = {
        tag = GRE
        date > 1940.1.1
        date < 1941.1.1
        ITA = {
            OR = {
                is_justifying_wargoal_against = GRE
                focus_progress = {
                    focus = ITA_greece_war_goal
                    progress > 0.01
                }
            }
        }
    }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { name = hellas.90.a hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hellas.91 days=3 } } }
}

country_event = {                                                                               ### Greece left Bulgarian border unmanned, make Bulgars declare war (mission -> ) 
	id = hellas.102
	title = hellas.102.t
	desc = hellas.102.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bul_military_parade_vidin

	trigger = {
        tag = GRE
        NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended }
        has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        OR = {
            ITA = { has_war_with = GRE }
            BUL = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
            BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
        }
        BUL = { 
            exists = yes
            NOT = { has_war_with = GRE } 
            OR = {
                NOT = { is_puppet_of = GRE }
                NOT = { is_subject_of = GRE }
            }
        }
        divisions_in_border_state = {
            type = infantry
            size < 3
            state = 812
            border_state = 212
        }     
        divisions_in_border_state = {
            type = infantry
            size < 1
            state = 731
            border_state = 212
        } 
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#Give into Greece
	option = {
		name = hellas.102.a

        activate_mission = GRE_reman_bulgarian_line
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                               ### Add infustructure to Albania, plus minor bases
	id = hellas.103
	title = hellas.103.t
	desc = hellas.103.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_italian_preparations

	trigger = {
        tag = GRE
        OR = {
            AND = {
                ALB = { exists = no }
                ITA = { 
                    controls_state = 44 
                    controls_state = 805
                }
            }
            AND = {
                ALB = { exists = yes }
                OR = {
                    is_puppet_of = ITA 
                    is_subject_of = ITA
                }
            }
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.103.a
        44 = {
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    is_controlled_by = ITA 
                    free_building_slots = {
                        building = infrastructure
                        size > 1
                        include_locked = yes
                    }
                }
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = infrastructure
                    level = 2
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
            add_building_construction = {
                type = air_base
                level = 1
                instant_build = yes
            }
            add_building_construction = {
                type = naval_base
                level = 2
                province = 11767
                instant_build = yes
            }
        }
        805 = {
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    is_controlled_by = ITA 
                    free_building_slots = {
                        building = infrastructure
                        size > 1
                        include_locked = yes
                    }
                }
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = infrastructure
                    level = 1
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
        }        
    }
}

	id = hellas.106
	title = hellas.106.t
	desc = hellas.106.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_italian_rise

	trigger = {
        original_tag = ITA
        has_war_with = GRE
        controls_state = 44
        date > 1941.3.8
    }

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.106.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }
        
        swap_ideas = { 
            remove_idea = GRE_italian_ambition
            add_idea = GRE_italian_ambition_ultra_offensive
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = { 
                GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_prepare_spring_offensive }
            }
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = ITA_spring_offensive
                days = 7
            }
        }
        else = {
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = ITA_spring_offensive
                days = 30
            }
        }
        
        GRE = { 
            country_event = { id = hellenic_news.152 days = 0 } 
            set_country_flag = GRE_italian_spring_offensive_started
        }
        
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Approach the Germans 
	id = hellas.109
	title = hellas.109.t
	desc = hellas.109.desc
	#picture = GFX_report_event_germany_politician_handshake

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {                                                                                      ## Germans Accept -> Toss the ball to the Italians 
		name = hellas.109.a
        
        ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 10
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
		}
        
        hidden_effect = {
            ITA = { country_event = { id = hellas.110 days = 0 }  }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Germans Decline (/continue war)
		name = hellas.109.b
        
        ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.5
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
		}
        
        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.112 days = 0 }  } 
    }
}

            modifier = {
