                check_variable = { var = ITA.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				check_variable = { var = ITA.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 1000
                GRE = { has_collaboration = { target = ITA value > 0.5} }

            modifier = {
                factor = 20
                check_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown > 0 }

            modifier = {
                factor = 5
                date < 1941.1.1
            }
		}

		}

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Greece managed to capilutate Bulgaria on time 
	id = hellas.113
	title = hellas.113.t
	desc = hellas.113.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bulgarslayer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                                      ## Annex if collaborative  
		name = hellas.113.a
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.45}
        }
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 3 }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.75}
            }
            annex_country = {
                target = BUL
                transfer_troops = yes
            }            
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.45}
            }
            annex_country = {
                target = BUL
                transfer_troops = no
            }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Make it integrated puppet
		name = hellas.113.b
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0}
            }
        }
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 2 }
        hidden_effect = {
            puppet = BUL
            set_autonomy = {
                target = BUL
                autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
            }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Keep as it is
		name = hellas.113.c
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 1 }
    }
}

                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_industrial = 2 } } ITA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_shackled_italian_industry_medium days = 180 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_industrial = 3 } } ITA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_shackled_italian_industry_high days = 180 } } }

                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_equipment = 2 } } ITA = { transfer_units_fraction = { target = GRE stockpile_ratio = 0.25 size = 0 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_equipment = 3 } } ITA = { transfer_units_fraction = { target = GRE stockpile_ratio = 0.50 size = 0 } } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_apology = 1 } } add_political_power = 500 }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_campaign = 1 } } ITA = { set_country_flag = domestic_pacification_campaign } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_apology = 1 } } ITA = { add_political_power = -150 add_stability = -0.2 add_war_support = -0.2 } }
                #####################[Future Stability]####################
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_guarantees = 1 } } every_country = { limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA } give_guarantee = GRE } set_global_flag = german_insurances_over_greece }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_non_agg = 1 } } ITA = { diplomatic_relation = { country = GRE relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes } set_global_flag = grecoitalian_non_aggression set_variable = { grecoitalian_na_renewal = 6 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_non_agg = 2 } } ITA = { diplomatic_relation = { country = GRE relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes } set_global_flag = grecoitalian_non_aggression set_variable = { grecoitalian_na_renewal = 9 } } }

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Metaxas Ribbentrop Pact Reply Event
	id = hellas.118
	title = {
        text = hellas.118_accepted.t
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    title = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected.t
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_accepted.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected1.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps < 2 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected2.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps = 2 } }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_metaxas_hitler
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
         ###[Calculate Success or Failure]###
            set_temp_variable = { multpl = 100 }                                            ### [Logic] 
            divide_temp_variable = { multpl = GRE.mr_negotiations_threshold }                 # Since the threshold is reduced based of inf/axal, we need to adjust the total rating to 100.
            set_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = GRE.mr_total_ratings }                     # Then we adjust the probabilities. Every point above 50 counts as 2. If we have >95, its 100%.
            multiply_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = multpl }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 50 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 2 }
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = adjusted_total
                min = 0
                max = 100
            }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { adjusted_total > 94.99 } } set_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 100 } }
            round_temp_variable = adjusted_total
            set_temp_variable = { cnter_chance = 100 }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { cnter_chance = adjusted_total }
            random_list = {
                log = yes
                seed = random
                var:adjusted_total = { set_temp_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
                var:cnter_chance = { set_temp_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
            }
         ###[Success Effects]###
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
                ###[Green Light for Naval Invasion]###
                set_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact
            }
        }
    }

	option = {
		name = hellas.118.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.118.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps < 2 } }
        add_to_variable = { mr_total_attemps = 1 }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.117 days = 0 } } }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.118.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
    }
}

                    limit = { 
                        is_controlled_by = GRE
                        is_core_of = ITA
                    }
                    add_compliance = 10
                }
            }
            ##[Border Limitations]##
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_demil_selected = 1 } } 
                every_state = {
                    limit = { 
                        NOT = { is_core_of = GRE } 
                        is_on_continent = europe
                        THIS.controller = { 
                            OR = {
                                tag = GRE
                                is_in_faction_with = GRE 
                                is_puppet_of = GRE
                                is_subject_of = GRE
                            }
                        }

                    every_neighbor_state = {

                            OR = {
                                is_controlled_by = GER
                                THIS.controller = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
                            }
                        }
                        PREV = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
                        add_to_variable = { GRE.mr_demil_selected_states = 1 }
                    }
                }
            }
            ###################[Basic Stuff]######################
            set_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_war
            set_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_big_war
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GER
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            }
            add_stability = 0.5
            add_war_support = 0.5
            news_event = { id = hellenic_news.154 }
            if = { limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_army } } country_event = { id = hellas.798 } }
            if = { limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_staff } } country_event = { id = hellas.799 } }
            complete_national_focus = GRE_the_weaves_of_fate
            set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
            clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.119.a
        clr_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact
        set_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact_Concluded
        MR_clear_variables = yes
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### PEACE ACHIEVED
	id = hellas.806
	title = hellas.806.t
	desc = hellas.806.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.806.a
         
        every_country = {
            limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
            white_peace = GRE
        }
        news_event = { id = hellenic_news.154 }
        complete_national_focus = GRE_the_weaves_of_fate
        complete_national_focus = GRE_glorious_struggle_in_triumph
        set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
        clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        if = { 
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_all_three_demanded }    
            GRE = { transfer_state = 44 }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }    
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_two_demanded }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }  
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_ne_demanded }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_dod_demanded }  
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }  
        }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_stockpile_and_units_disbanded }    
            BUL = { 
                #teleport_armies = { to_state = 48 } 
                delete_unit = {
                    state = 48
                    disband = yes
                }
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 1
                    stockpile_ratio = 1
                    army_ratio = 1
                    navy_ratio = 1
                    air_ratio = 1
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_stockpile }
            BUL = {
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 1
                    stockpile_ratio = 1
                    army_ratio = 0
                    navy_ratio = 0
                    air_ratio = 0
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_units_disbanded }
            BUL = { 
                #teleport_armies = { to_state = 48 } 
                delete_unit = { 
                    state = 48
                    disband = yes
                }
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 0
                    stockpile_ratio = 0.5
                    army_ratio = 0
                    navy_ratio = 0
                    air_ratio = 0
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

                    }

country_event = {                                                                                
	id = hellas.1003
	title = hellas.1003.t
	desc = hellas.1003.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hellenic_state

	is_triggered_only = yes 
    
	fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_global_flag = monthly_favor_mechanic_frozen
            set_global_flag = GRE_hellenic_state_formed
            set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
            set_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding
            clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
            create_dynamic_country = {
                original_tag = GRE
                save_global_event_target_as = hellenic_state
                #save_event_target_as = hellenic_state
                every_state = { #transfer to HS
                    limit = {
                        is_owned_by = GRE
                        NOT = { state = 182 }
                    }
                    event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = PREV }
                }
                #############################[Setup Occupation Zones]############################
                813 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                731 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                811 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                810 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                47 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                187 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                807 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                808 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                809 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                186 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                185 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                814 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                #######################[Bulgarian Direct Annexations (Historical)]###############
                if = {                                                                                                              # If Bulgaria is alive, in Axis and historical stuff should happen.
                    limit = {
                        BUL = {
                            exists = yes
                            OR = {
                                is_in_faction_with = GER
                                is_in_faction_with = ITA
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    731 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    731 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    731 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    811 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    811 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    811 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }   
                    813 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    813 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    813 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }                
                    184 = { BUL = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                    812 = { BUL = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                }
                else = {
                    184 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }                                      # Italians take control of their portion, as this would have happened historically since the Germans only took strategic regions and Italians the mass of land.
                    812 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                }
                ################################[Rule Setting]###################################
                set_rule = { 
                    can_join_factions = no 
                    can_create_factions = no
                    can_not_declare_war = yes
                    can_send_volunteers = no
                }
                #GER = { add_to_faction = event_target:hellenic_state }             # Not a good idea because GRE will be able to see all Axis troops., so just give access (below)
                GER = { transfer_state = 47 }                                       # TEMPORARILY TO NAVAL INVADE CRETE (doesn't work otherwise)
                GER = { transfer_state = 811 }    
                set_capital = 47
                set_politics = {
                    ruling_party = fascism
                    elections_allowed = no
                }
                set_popularities = {
                    democratic = 15
                    fascism = 50
                    neutrality = 20
                    communism = 15
                }
                set_cosmetic_tag = GRE_HELLENIC_STATE_fascism
                create_country_leader = {
                    name = "Geórgios Tsolákoglou"
                    desc = "POLITICS_GEORGIOS_TSOLAKOGLOU_DESC"
                    picture = "Portrait_Greece_Georgios_Tsolakoglou.dds"
                    expire = "1965.1.1"
                    ideology = fascism_ideology
                    traits = {
                        
                    }
                }
                GRE = {                                                                     ## Disband Units in Aegean Islands and mainland Greece
                    delete_unit = {state = 807 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 47 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 186 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 187 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 814 disband = yes}
                    set_temp_variable = { convoy_num = GRE.convoys_secured }
                    multiply_temp_variable = { convoy_num = -1 }
                    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                        type = convoy_1
                        amount = convoy_num
                        producer = GRE
                    }
                    transfer_units_fraction = {                                             ## Germany takes 75% of stockpile from virtually SURRENDERED troops
                        target = GER                                                         # This is why evacuated divisions will retain equipment, while disbanded (see above) will put eq to stockpile.
                        size = 0                                                             # So basically the 25% left is what you """evacuated""" to Crete.
                        stockpile_ratio = 0.75
                        army_ratio = 0
                        navy_ratio = 0.0
                        air_ratio = 0.0
                        keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                            always = yes
                        }
                    }
                }
                inherit_technology = GRE
                set_research_slots = 0
                add_ideas = HS_ind_shackles_4
                add_ideas = HS_tripple_occupation
                add_ideas = HS_occupation_costs
                add_ideas = HS_german_plundering
                add_ideas = HS_death
                if = {
                    limit = { GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } }
                    add_ideas = HS_spirit_of_grand_coalition
                }
                load_focus_tree = hellenic_state_focus
                GRE = { GR_HS_split_ideas = yes }
                #GER = { puppet = event_target:hellenic_state }
                complete_national_focus = glorious_struggle_in_vain
                complete_national_focus = hellenic_state
                complete_national_focus = appoint_tsolakoglou
            }
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_faction_with = GER
                }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = non_aggression_pact
                    active = yes
                }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = military_access
                    active = yes
                }
            }
            GER = {
                add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_german_ambition_crete days = 60 }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = guarantee
                    active = yes
                }
                remove_ideas = GRE_german_ambition
            }
            ITA = {
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = guarantee
                    active = yes
                }
            }
            HS_set_up_occupation_zones = yes
            HS_calculate_factories_in_occupation_zones = yes
            HS_flag_states = yes 
            #######[Resource Rights for Sterea/Pel. go to the Reich]######
            ITA = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 807 } }
            ITA = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 186 } }
            ##############################################################
            GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.1004 days = 10 } }
        }
    }
	
	option = {                                                                            
		name = hellas.1003.a
    }
}

            is_in_array = {
                array = global.greek_mainland_states_all
                value = THIS
            }
        }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
        days = 180
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.25
            OR = {
                state = 47
                state = 811
            }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.50
            OR = {
                state = 808
                state = 187
            }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.75
            OR = {
                state = 182
                state = 186
                state = 807
            }
        }
    }

	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            GRE = { add_political_power = 100 }
            THIS = { event_based_black_market_shift = yes }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                
	id = hellas.10000
	title = hellas.10000.t
	desc = {                                                                                        ## Crete did not fall
        text = hellas.10000a.desc
        trigger = {
            GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_holds }
        }
    }
    desc = {                                                                                        ## Crete fell
        text = hellas.10000b.desc
        trigger = {
            GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_falls }
        }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_germany_politician_handshake

	#trigger = {
    #    original_tag = GRE
    #    is_ai = no
    #    date > 1941.06.15
    #    event_target:hellenic_state = { NOT = { controls_state = 47 } }
    #}
    
    is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                            
		name = hellas.10000.a
        
        event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 47 }
        event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 811 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 11818 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 4109 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 11965 }
        47 = { add_resistance = 6 }
        if = {
            limit = { GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_falls } }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 270 }
            event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 182 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 12058 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 1164 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 9940 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 4170 }
            add_to_array = { global.greek_mainland_states_all = 182 }
            add_to_array = { global.german_occupied_states = 182 }
            182 = { 
                add_resistance = 9 
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = unyielding_greeks_angered }
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone }
            }
            HS_calculate_factories_in_occupation_zones = yes
            country_event = { id = hellas.1007 days = 0 }
        }
        else = {
            country_event = { id = hellas.1006 days = 0 }
        }
    }
}
